    <script data-ot-ignore>
  const SEGMENT_DATA = {
    customer: {
      id: '',
      email: '',
      first_name: '',
      last_name: '',
    },
  }

  window.Segment = {
    debug: Boolean(localStorage && localStorage.getItem('segment.debug')),

    init() {},

    centsToMoney(cents) {
      return ((parseFloat(`${cents}`) || 0) / 100).toFixed(2)
    },

    getContext() {
      const email = SEGMENT_DATA.customer.email

      return email
        ? {
            externalIds: [
              {
                id: SEGMENT_DATA.customer.email,
                type: 'email',
                collection: 'users',
                encoding: 'none',
              },
            ],
          }
        : {}
    },

    getTargetingCookiesAllowed() {
      const reduceQueryToObject = (object, part) => {
        const [key, ...values] = part.split(/\s*=\s*/)
        object[key] = decodeURIComponent(values.join('='))
        return object
      }
      const cookies = document.cookie
        .split(/\s*;\s*/)
        .reduce(reduceQueryToObject, {})

      const consentCookie = cookies.OptanonConsent || null
      if (!consentCookie) return true

      const consentData = consentCookie
        .split('&')
        .reduce(reduceQueryToObject, {})
      if (!consentData) return false

      const groups = consentData.groups || null
      const targetingCookieGroup = 'C0004'

      return groups ? groups.includes(`${targetingCookieGroup}:1`) : false
    },

    validate() {
      if (!this.getTargetingCookiesAllowed()) {
        console.warn('Analytics not allowed')
        return false
      }

      if (typeof window.analytics === 'undefined') {
        console.warn('Analytics not enabled')
        return false
      }

      return true
    },

    async getUser() {
      if (!this.validate()) {
        return null
      }

      return await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        analytics.ready(() => {
          resolve(analytics.user())
        })
      })
    },

    track(event, properties = {}) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugTrack(event, properties)
      analytics.track(event, properties, this.getContext())
    },

    debugTrack(event, properties = {}) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics event fired`, {
        event,
        properties,
      })
    },

    identify(userId = null, traits) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugIdentify(userId, traits)

      if (userId) {
        analytics.identify(userId, traits)
      } else {
        analytics.identify(traits)
      }
    },

    debugIdentify(userId, traits) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics identify fired`, {
        userId,
        traits,
      })
    },

    alias(customerId, previousId) {
      if (!this.validate()) return

      this.debugAlias(userId, previousId)

      analytics.alias(userId, previousId)
    },

    debugAlias(userId, previousId) {
      if (!this.debug) return

      console.log(`Analytics alias fired`, {
        userId,
        previousId,
      })
    },
  }

  window.onload = Segment.init()
</script>

var translateTextNode = function(node) {
if(node.textContent && node.textContent.trim().length > 0) {
var src = node.textContent.trim().replace(/(\r\n|\n|\r)/gm,"").replace(/\s+/g," ").toUpperCase();
if(customContents[src] && node.textContent !== customContents[src]) {
var newContent = node.textContent.replace(node.textContent.trim(), customContents[src]); if (newContent != node.textContent) { node.textContent = newContent }
}
}
}
try {var textNodes = $('body').find('*').addBack().not('script').not('style').contents().filter(function() {
if(this.nodeType === 3) {
translateTextNode(this);
}
});
} catch(e) {};var target = document.querySelector('body');
var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
var newNodes = mutation.addedNodes;
if(newNodes) {
for(i = 0; i < newNodes.length; i++) {
try {var textNodes = $(newNodes[i]).find('*').addBack().not('script').not('style').contents().filter(function() {
if(this.nodeType === 3) {
translateTextNode(this);
}
});
} catch(e) {};}
}
if(mutation.type === 'characterData') {
translateTextNode(mutation.target);
}
});
});
var config = { childList: true, characterData: true, subtree: true }
observer.observe(target, config);

var LySwitcherDrawer = LySwitcherDrawer || {
  templateList: new Array(),
  init: function() {
    LySwitcherDrawer._fetchDrawerData();
    setTimeout(function() {
      for(var i=0; i<LySwitcherDrawer.templateList.length; i++) {
        var template = LySwitcherDrawer.templateList[i];

        if(template.target){
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find(template.target);
        } else {
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find('a[href="/cart"], a[href="#cart"], .cart-toggle, .site-header__cart');
        }

        $orientationTargets.each(function() {
          LySwitcherDrawer._draw(template, $(this));
        });
      }
      LySwitcherDrawer._bindSwitcherEvents();
    }, 500);
  },
  _fetchDrawerData: function() {
    var me = this;
    $('.ly-drawer-template').each(function(i) {
      me.templateList.push({
        id: i,
        align: $(this).data('align'),
        target: $(this).data('target'),
        targetIsContainer: $(this).data('target-is-container'),
        type: $(this).data('type'),
        css: $(this).data('css'),
        class: $(this).data('class'),
        template: $(this).html()
      });
      $(this).remove();
    });
  },


  _draw: function(template, $orientationTarget) {
    var $switcherElem = null;
    var switcherHtml = template.template;
    var $target = $orientationTarget;
    if(template.targetIsContainer === true) {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.prepend(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      }
    } else {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.before(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      }
    }
    $switcherElem.find('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher, .ly-languages-links-switcher, .ly-languages-links-icons-switcher').attr('style', template.css);
  },
  _bindSwitcherEvents: function() {
    $('.ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher').click(function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var dropdownList = $(this).find('ul');
      if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
        dropdownList.css('bottom', $(this).outerHeight());
      } else {
        dropdownList.css('top', $(this).outerHeight());
      }
      if($(this).hasClass('ly-is-open')) {
        $(this).removeClass('ly-is-open');
        dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:none !important;')
      } else {
        $(this).addClass('ly-is-open');
        if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;bottom:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        } else {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;top:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        }
      }
    });
    $('.ly-languages-link').click(function (e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage(this.id);
    });
    $('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown').change(function(e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage($(this).val());
    });
  },
};

        edit_address: '編輯地址',
        view_all_orders: '查看所有訂單',
        reset_cookies_title: '重設 Cookies',
        reset_cookies_action: '重設 Cookies',
        reset_cookies_info: '這項作業將會刪除所有跟您的帳號關聯的瀏覽歷史',
      },
      address_form: {
        personal_details: '個人資訊',
        first_name: '名',
        last_name: '姓',
        phone: '電話',

        address: '地址',
        province: '省',
        city: '市',
        country: '國家',
        postal_code: '郵遞區號',
        set_as_default: '設為預設值',
        save: '儲存',
        cancel: '取消',
        select_province: '選擇您的省/市',
        first_name_error: '缺少名字資訊',
        last_name_error: '缺少姓名資訊',
        city_error: '缺少城市資訊',
        address_error: '缺少地址資訊',
        province_error: '缺少省/市資訊',
        postal_code_error: '缺少郵遞區號資訊',
      },
    },
  };

  /**
   * Current language translations.
   */
  const getCurrentTranslations = () => ({...translations[currentLang] ?? translations['en']});

  return {
    currentLang,

    /**
    * Current language translations.
    */
    t: getCurrentTranslations(),

    /**
    * Used to get translations that have a variable placeholder.
    */
    tArg: (translationKey, value, ndValue) => {
      const variablePlaceholder = '{n}'
      const ndVariablePlaceholder = '{k}'

      const translationKeys = translationKey.split('.')
      let result = getCurrentTranslations();

      for (const key of translationKeys) {
        result = result[key]
      }

      if (!result || typeof result !== 'string') {
        console.error('Cannot find translation for: ', translationKey)
        return ''
      }

      if (!result.includes(variablePlaceholder)) {
        console.error('Translation string does not have variable slot: ', translationKey)
        return ''
      }

      const first = result.replace(variablePlaceholder, value)

      if (ndValue) {
        return first.replace(ndVariablePlaceholder, ndValue)
      }

      return first;
    },
  };
})();

    <script type="text/x-template" id="cart-product-item">
  <div class="cart-product-item">
    <div class="item-image">
      <template v-if="url">
        <a :href="url">
          <img :src="image">
        </a>
      </template>
      <template v-else>
        <img :src="image">
      </template>
      <div class="item-image-price" v-show="hideDetails" v-html="$root.formatMoney(finalPrice, false)"></div>
    </div>
    <div class="item-details" v-show="!hideDetails">
      <div class="item-title">
        <template v-if="url">
          <a :href="url">
            ${title}
          </a>
        </template>
        <template v-else>
          ${title}
        </template>
      </div>
      <div class="item-price" v-html="$root.formatMoney(finalPrice, false)"></div>
      <slot></slot>
    </div>
    <div class="item-qty-controls" :class="{ 'disabled': disabled }">
      <template v-if="quantity === 0">
        <div class="qty-control qty-cart" @click="increaseQty">
          <img class="icon icon-cart" :src="$root.asset('icon-add-to-cart.svg')">
        </div>
      </template>
      <template v-else>
        <div
          class="qty-control qty-plus"
          :class="{ 'disabled': !canIncreaseQty }"
          @click="increaseQty"
        >
          &plus;
        </div>
        <div class="qty-control qty-amount">
          <input
            maxlength="4"
            :value="localQuantity"
            @blur="updateQtyFromInput"
            @keyup.enter="updateQtyFromInput"
          >
        </div>
        <div
          class="qty-control qty-minus"
          :class="{ 'disabled': !canDecreaseQty }"
          @click="decreaseQty"
        >
          &ndash;
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
  </div>
</script>

<script>Vue.component("cart-product-item",{template:"#cart-product-item",props:{id:Number,title:String,image:String,price:Number,quantity:Number,disabled:Boolean,url:String,hideDetails:Boolean},data(){return{limit:{},isLimitEnabled:!1,cartUpdateTimeout:null,cartUpdateDelay:500,localQuantity:this.quantity}},delimiters:["${","}"],watch:{quantity(t){this.localQuantity=t}},computed:{finalPrice(){return this.quantity>0?this.price*this.quantity:this.price},productId(){const t=CartJS.cart.items.find(t=>t.id===this.id);return t&&parseInt(t.product_id)},canIncreaseQty(){return!(this.localQuantity>=9999)&&(!this.isLimitEnabled||this.localQuantity<this.limit.max)},canDecreaseQty(){return this.localQuantity>0}},methods:{async setLimit(){const t=(await this.$root.getCustomerProductLimits()).some(t=>t.variantId===this.id);t&&(this.limit=t,this.isLimitEnabled=!0)},updateQuantity(t,i){this.disabled||(clearTimeout(this.cartUpdateTimeout),this.cartUpdateTimeout=setTimeout(()=>{CartJS.updateItemQuantitiesById({[t]:i})},this.cartUpdateDelay))},increaseQty(){this.canIncreaseQty&&(this.localQuantity++,this.updateQuantity(this.id,this.localQuantity))},decreaseQty(){this.canDecreaseQty&&(this.localQuantity--,this.updateQuantity(this.id,this.localQuantity))},updateQtyFromInput(t){const{value:i}=t.target,a=parseInt(i);a>=0?a!==this.localQuantity&&this.updateQuantity(this.id,a):t.target.value=this.quantity}},created(){this.setLimit()}});</script>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">Vue.component("product-bisn",{template:"#product-bisn",delimiters:["${","}"],props:{customerId:[Number,String],email:String,productId:[Number,String],sku:String,hideAdditionalText:{type:Boolean,default:!1}},data:()=>({t:TRANSLATIONS.t,apiUrl:"/apps/shop-manager/api",subscribed:!1,loading:!1}),computed:{isLoggedIn(){return this.customerId>0}},methods:{getRequestData(){const{shop:s}=Shopify,{customerId:t,email:e,productId:i,sku:r}=this.$props;return{shop:s,customerId:`${t}`,email:e,productId:`${i}`,sku:r,subscribe:this.subscribed}},async sendPostRequest(s,t){const e=await fetch(s,{method:"POST",headers:{Accept:"application/json","Content-Type":"application/json"},body:JSON.stringify(t)});return 200===e.status&&e.json()},async checkIfSubscribed(){this.loading=!0;const s=await this.sendPostRequest(`${this.apiUrl}/bisn/subscribed`,this.getRequestData());this.subscribed=!!s,this.loading=!1},async onCheckboxChange(){this.loading=!0,this.subscribed=!this.subscribed;try{if(!await this.sendPostRequest(`${this.apiUrl}/bisn`,this.getRequestData()))throw new Error}catch(s){this.subscribed=!this.subscribed}this.loading=!1}},created(){this.checkIfSubscribed()}});</script>

<script data-ot-ignore type="text/javascript">Vue.component("horizontal-loader",{props:{classes:{type:String,default:""}},template:"#horizontal-loader",delimiters:["${","}"]});</script>

<style scoped>.circleG-wrapper{width:90px;display:flex;justify-content:center;align-items:center;margin:auto}.circleG{background-color:#fff;height:8px;width:8px;margin:0 6px;animation-name:bounce_circleG;-o-animation-name:bounce_circleG;-ms-animation-name:bounce_circleG;-webkit-animation-name:bounce_circleG;-moz-animation-name:bounce_circleG;animation-duration:2s;-o-animation-duration:2s;-ms-animation-duration:2s;-webkit-animation-duration:2s;-moz-animation-duration:2s;animation-iteration-count:infinite;-o-animation-iteration-count:infinite;-ms-animation-iteration-count:infinite;-webkit-animation-iteration-count:infinite;-moz-animation-iteration-count:infinite;animation-direction:normal;-o-animation-direction:normal;-ms-animation-direction:normal;-webkit-animation-direction:normal;-moz-animation-direction:normal;border-radius:px;-o-border-radius:20px;-ms-border-radius:20px;-webkit-border-radius:20px;-moz-border-radius:20px}.circleG_1{animation-delay:0s;-o-animation-delay:0s;-ms-animation-delay:0s;-webkit-animation-delay:0s;-moz-animation-delay:0s}.circleG_2{animation-delay:.4s;-o-animation-delay:.6s;-ms-animation-delay:.6s;-webkit-animation-delay:.6s;-moz-animation-delay:.6s}.circleG_3{animation-delay:8s;-o-animation-delay:1.05s;-ms-animation-delay:1.05s;-webkit-animation-delay:1.05s;-moz-animation-delay:1.05s}@keyframes bounce_circleG{50%{background-color:rgb(255,255,255,0)}}@-o-keyframes bounce_circleG{50%{background-color:rgb(255,255,255,0)}}@-ms-keyframes bounce_circleG{50%{background-color:rgb(255,255,255,0)}}@-webkit-keyframes bounce_circleG{50%{background-color:rgb(255,255,255,0)}}@-moz-keyframes bounce_circleG{50%{background-color:rgb(255,255,255,0)}}</style>

    
    <div id="app">
      <cart-banner
        :show="isCartBannerShown"
      ></cart-banner>
      <cart-modal
        :open="isCartModalOpen"
        :cart-accessories="appData.cartAccessories"
        v-on:close="closeCart"
      ></cart-modal>
    </div>

    <script>
      const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',

        i18n,

        data() {
          return {
            appData: window.APP_DATA || {},
            isCartModalOpen: false,
            isCartBannerShown: false,
            breakpoints: {
              MOBILE: 480,
              TABLET: 768,
              LAPTOP: 960,
              DESKTOP: 1200,
            },
            isMobileResolution: false,
            isTabletResolution: false,
            defaultQtyMinimum: 0,
            defaultQtyMaximum: 50,
            customerProductLimits: null,
            decimalSeparator: '.',
            thousandsSeparator: ',',
            currentLang: localeCodes[langify.helper.getSelectedLanguage()],
          };
        },

        methods: {
          /**
           * Return unique array values
           *
           * @returns {Array}
           */
           onlyUnique(value, index, self) {
            return self.indexOf(value) === index;
          },

          /**
           * @returns {Object[]}
           */
          getBoughtItemQtiesGroupedBySku() {
            const boughtItems = this.appData.boughtItems;
            const boughtItemQties = {};

            for (const { sku, qty } of boughtItems) {
              const oldQty = boughtItemQties[sku] || 0;

              boughtItemQties[sku] = oldQty + qty;
            }

            return boughtItemQties;
          },

          /**
           * Group GET request parameters as an object
           *
           * @returns {Object}
           */
          searchParams() {
            const paramsMap = window.location.search
              .replace('?', '')
              .split('&')
              .map(param => param.split('='));

            // Convert the params map to an object
            const params = {};

            for (const [key, value] of paramsMap) {
              params[key] = value;
            }

            return params;
          },

          /**
           * Set resolution booleans
           */
          checkResolutions() {
            const ww = window.outerWidth;

            this.isMobileResolution = ww <= this.breakpoints.MOBILE;
            this.isTabletResolution = ww <= this.breakpoints.TABLET;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to fetch asset with typecheck
           */
          asset(key, fallback = null) {
            const asset = this.appData.assets[key];

            return typeof asset !== 'undefined' ? asset : fallback;
          },

          /**
           * Open the cart modal
           */
          openCart() {
            this.isCartModalOpen = true;
          },

          /**
           * Close the cart modal
           */
          closeCart() {
            this.isCartModalOpen = false;
          },

          /**
           * Show the cart banner
           */
          showCartBanner() {
            this.isCartBannerShown = true;
          },

          /**
           * Hide the cart banner
           */
          hideCartBanner() {
            this.isCartBannerShown = false;
          },

          /**
           * Helper method to format money
           *
           * @param {number} cents
           * @param {applyVat} boolean
           * @param {withDecimals} boolean
           * @returns {string}
           */
          formatMoney(cents, applyVat = false) {
            // Format money
            const money = Shopify.formatMoney(cents, false, applyVat)
            const parts = money.split(' ')
            const moneyPart = parts[0].split(
              this.decimalSeparator,
            )

            const primary = moneyPart[0]
            const decimal = moneyPart[1] || ''
            const suffix = parts[1] || ''

            // Combine parts to render
            const html = [`<span>${primary}</span>`]

            if (decimal) {
              html.push(`<span class="smaller">${this.decimalSeparator}${decimal}</span>`)
            }
            if (suffix) {
              html.push(`&nbsp;<span>${suffix}</span>`)
            }

            return html.join('')
          },

          formatMoneySimple(cents, applyVat = false) {
            // Format money
            const money = Shopify.formatMoney(cents, false, applyVat)
            const parts = money.split(' ')
            const moneyPart = parts[0].split(
              this.decimalSeparator,
            )

            const primary = moneyPart[0]
            const decimal = moneyPart[1] || ''
            const suffix = parts[1] || ''

            // Combine parts to render
            const html = [`${primary}`]

            if (decimal) {
              html.push(`${this.decimalSeparator}${decimal}`)
            }
            if (suffix) {
              html.push(`&nbsp;${suffix}`)
            }

            return html.join('')
          },

          /**
           * Set-up all cart related actions
           */
          initCart() {
            // Initiate CartJS
            CartJS.init(this.appData.cart, {
              'requestBodyClass': 'loading',
              'moneyFormat': 'TWD {{amount}}',
              'moneyWithCurrencyFormat': 'TWD {{amount}}'
            });

            // Open the cart if requested
            if (window.location.search === "?cart") {
              window.history.replaceState({}, null, window.location.pathname);
              this.openCart();
            }

            // Handle cart header menu item
            jQuery(document).on('click', '.site-header__cart-toggle', e => {
              e.preventDefault();
              this.openCart();
            });
          },

          setProductSku() {
            const { product } = this.appData;
            const { variant: variantId } = this.searchParams();
            const skuEl = document.querySelector('.product-current-sku');

            if (product && skuEl) {
              // Use the first variant by default
              let variant = product.variants[0];

              if (variantId) {
                // Find the variant based on the request parameter
                variant = product.variants.find(
                  variant => parseInt(variant.id) === parseInt(variantId)
                );
              }

              if (variant) {
                // Update the SKU
                let gen2 = new RegExp('-gen2', 'i');
                let disabled = new RegExp('-disabled', 'i');
                let standalone = new RegExp('-Standalone', 'i');
                let beta = new RegExp('-BETA', 'i');
                skuEl.innerText = variant.sku.replace(gen2, '')
                  .replace(disabled, '')
                  .replace(standalone, '')
                  .replace(beta, '-EA');
              }
            }
          },

          makeSlug(text) {
            return text.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/-$/, '').replace(/^-/, '');
          },

          getUrlParameter(sParam) {
            const sPageURL = decodeURIComponent(window.location.search.substring(1))
            const sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&')

            for (const variable of sURLVariables) {
              const [key, value] = variable.split('=')

              if (key === sParam) {
                return typeof value === 'undefined' ? true : value
              }
            }
          },

          replaceUrlParam(e,r,a){
            var n=new RegExp("("+r+"=).*?(&|$)"),c=e;return c=e.search(n)>=0?e.replace(n,"$1"+a+"$2"):c+(c.indexOf("?")>0?"&":"?")+r+"="+a
          },

          /**
           * Handle [data-toggle] that toggles [data-toggle-id] elements
           */
          handleDataToggle(e) {
            const $action = jQuery(e.currentTarget);
            const targetId = $action.data('toggle');
            const $target = jQuery(`[data-toggle-id="${targetId}"]`);

            const toggleText = $action.attr('data-toggle-text');
            const toggleTextNew = $action.attr('data-toggle-text-new');
            const toggleTextTarget = $action.children('[data-toggle-text-target]').first();

            const forceOpen = typeof $action.data('toggle-open') !== 'undefined';
            const forceClose = typeof $action.data('toggle-close') !== 'undefined' && !forceOpen;

            e.preventDefault();

            if ($action.hasClass('active') || forceClose) {
              if (!forceOpen) {
                $target.removeClass('active');
                $target.stop(true).slideUp(300);
                $action.removeClass('active');
              }
            } else if (!$action.hasClass('active') || forceOpen) {
              if (!forceClose) {
                $target.addClass('active');
                $target.stop(true).slideDown(300);
                $action.addClass('active');
              }
            }

            if(!!toggleText && !!toggleTextNew && !!toggleTextTarget) {
              $action.hasClass('active') ? toggleTextTarget.text(toggleTextNew) : toggleTextTarget.text(toggleText);
            }

          },

          /**
           * Handle [data-scroll-to] that scrolls to [data-scroll-to-id] elements
           */
          handleDataScrollTo(e) {
            const $action = jQuery(e.currentTarget);
            const targetId = $action.data('scroll-to');
            const $target = jQuery(`[data-scroll-to-id="${targetId}"]`);

            jQuery('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: $target.offset().top,
            }, 600);
          },

          /**
           * Fetch and parse a cart attribute
           *
           * @param {string} name
           * @returns {Object}
           */
          getCartAttribute(name) {
            const attributes = CartJS.getAttributes();
            const attribute = attributes && attributes[name] ? attributes[name] : '{}';

            return JSON.parse(attribute.replace(/=>/g, ':'));
          },

          /**
           * @param {boolean} forceUpdate
           * @returns {Promise<{ sku: string; max: string }[]>}
           */
          async getCustomerProductLimits(forceUpdate = false) {
            if (!this.customerProductLimits || forceUpdate) {
              const response = await fetch('/apps/shop-manager/api/product-limits', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                  Accept: 'application/json',
                  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({ shop: Shopify.shop }),
              })

              try {
                this.customerProductLimits = await response.json();
              } catch (error) {
                console.error(error)
                this.customerProductLimits = [];
              }

            }

            return this.customerProductLimits;
          },

          /**
           * Handle login referral redirect
           *
           * @returns {void}
           */
          handleLoginReferral() {
            if (!localStorage) {
              return
            }

            // If referral exists and not on login page
            const accountLoginRef = localStorage.getItem('account-login-ref')
            const isLoginPage = location.pathname === '/account/login'

            if (!accountLoginRef || isLoginPage) {
              return
            }

            // Remove the item
            localStorage.removeItem('account-login-ref')

            // Only if on account page (after login)
            const isAccountPage = location.pathname === '/account'

            if (!isAccountPage) {
              return
            }

            // Redirect to the referred url
            window.location = accountLoginRef
          },

          redirectToLogin() {
            // Set a local storage referral url to current page
            if (localStorage) {
              localStorage.setItem('account-login-ref', location.href)
            }
            // Redirect
            location.href = '/account/login';
          },
        },

        created() {
          this.checkResolutions();
          this.initCart();
        },

        mounted() {
          this.setProductSku();
          this.handleLoginReferral()

          // Events
          jQuery(() => {
            // Show cart banner when document is loaded
            this.isCartBannerShown = true
            this.setProductSku();
          })
          jQuery(window).on('resize', this.checkResolutions);
          jQuery(document).on('click', '[data-toggle]', this.handleDataToggle);
          jQuery(document).on('click', '[data-scroll-to]', this.handleDataScrollTo);

          // pushState event hack
          const pushState = history.pushState;
          history.pushState = (...args) => {
            pushState.apply(history, args);

            // Custom events
            this.setProductSku();
          };
        },
      });
    </script>

var translateTextNode = function(node) {
if(node.textContent && node.textContent.trim().length > 0) {
var src = node.textContent.trim().replace(/(\r\n|\n|\r)/gm,"").replace(/\s+/g," ").toUpperCase();
if(customContents[src] && node.textContent !== customContents[src]) {
var newContent = node.textContent.replace(node.textContent.trim(), customContents[src]); if (newContent != node.textContent) { node.textContent = newContent }
}
}
}
try {var textNodes = $('body').find('*').addBack().not('script').not('style').contents().filter(function() {
if(this.nodeType === 3) {
translateTextNode(this);
}
});
} catch(e) {};var target = document.querySelector('body');
var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
var newNodes = mutation.addedNodes;
if(newNodes) {
for(i = 0; i < newNodes.length; i++) {
try {var textNodes = $(newNodes[i]).find('*').addBack().not('script').not('style').contents().filter(function() {
if(this.nodeType === 3) {
translateTextNode(this);
}
});
} catch(e) {};}
}
if(mutation.type === 'characterData') {
translateTextNode(mutation.target);
}
});
});
var config = { childList: true, characterData: true, subtree: true }
observer.observe(target, config);

  init: function() {
    LySwitcherDrawer._fetchDrawerData();
    setTimeout(function() {
      for(var i=0; i<LySwitcherDrawer.templateList.length; i++) {
        var template = LySwitcherDrawer.templateList[i];

        if(template.target){
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find(template.target);
        } else {
          var $orientationTargets = $('body').find('a[href="/cart"], a[href="#cart"], .cart-toggle, .site-header__cart');
        }

        $orientationTargets.each(function() {
          LySwitcherDrawer._draw(template, $(this));
        });
      }
      LySwitcherDrawer._bindSwitcherEvents();
    }, 500);
  },
  _fetchDrawerData: function() {
    var me = this;
    $('.ly-drawer-template').each(function(i) {
      me.templateList.push({
        id: i,
        align: $(this).data('align'),
        target: $(this).data('target'),
        targetIsContainer: $(this).data('target-is-container'),
        type: $(this).data('type'),
        css: $(this).data('css'),
        class: $(this).data('class'),
        template: $(this).html()
      });
      $(this).remove();
    });
  },


  _draw: function(template, $orientationTarget) {
    var $switcherElem = null;
    var switcherHtml = template.template;
    var $target = $orientationTarget;
    if(template.targetIsContainer === true) {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.prepend(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.append(switcherHtml);
      }
    } else {
      if(template.align === 'left') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.before(switcherHtml);
      } else if(template.align === 'right') {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      } else {
        $switcherElem = $orientationTarget.after(switcherHtml);
      }
    }
    $switcherElem.find('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher, .ly-languages-links-switcher, .ly-languages-links-icons-switcher').attr('style', template.css);
  },
  _bindSwitcherEvents: function() {
    $('.ly-languages-image-dropdown-switcher, .ly-languages-image-dropdown-icons-switcher').click(function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var dropdownList = $(this).find('ul');
      if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
        dropdownList.css('bottom', $(this).outerHeight());
      } else {
        dropdownList.css('top', $(this).outerHeight());
      }
      if($(this).hasClass('ly-is-open')) {
        $(this).removeClass('ly-is-open');
        dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:none !important;')
      } else {
        $(this).addClass('ly-is-open');
        if($(this).data('dropup') === true) {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;bottom:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        } else {
          dropdownList.attr('style', 'display:inline-block !important;top:' + $(this).outerHeight() + 'px')
        }
      }
    });
    $('.ly-languages-link').click(function (e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage(this.id);
    });
    $('.ly-languages-switcher-dropdown').change(function(e) {
      langify.helper.saveLanguage($(this).val());
    });
  },
};

          url: 'https://store.ui.com',
          name: 'USA Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.US],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-canada.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://ca.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Canada Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.CA],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-japan.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://jp.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Japan Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.JP],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-mexico.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://mx.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Mexico Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.MX],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-india.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://in.store.ui.com',
          name: 'India Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.IN],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-taiwan.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://tw.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Taiwan Store',
          countries: [COUNTRY.TW],
        },
        {
          origin: 'store-ui-europe.myshopify.com',
          url: 'https://eu.store.ui.com',
          name: 'Europe Store',
          countries: [
            COUNTRY.AT,
            COUNTRY.BE,
            COUNTRY.BG,
            COUNTRY.HR,
            COUNTRY.CZ,
            COUNTRY.DK,
            COUNTRY.EE,
            COUNTRY.FI,
            COUNTRY.FR,
            COUNTRY.DE,
            COUNTRY.EL,
            COUNTRY.ES,
            COUNTRY.HU,
            COUNTRY.IE,
            COUNTRY.IT,
            COUNTRY.LV,
            COUNTRY.LT,
            COUNTRY.LU,
            COUNTRY.NL,
            COUNTRY.PL,
            COUNTRY.PT,
            COUNTRY.RO,
            COUNTRY.SK,
            COUNTRY.SI,
            COUNTRY.SE,
            COUNTRY.CH,
            COUNTRY.UK,
          ],
        },
        {
          origin: "me.store.ui.com",
          url: "https://me.store.ui.com",
          name: "Middle East Store",
          countries: [COUNTRY.AE],
        },
      ],
      cookieKey: 'geo-select',
      canShow: false,
    }
  },

  computed: {
    hasCurrencySelect() {
      const shopOrigins = ['store-ui-europe.myshopify.com']

      return this.shop !== null && shopOrigins.includes(this.shop.origin)
    },

    currencySelectCurrencies() {
      const result = []

      if (this.hasCurrencySelect) {
        for (const { currency } of this.shop.countries) {
          if (!result.includes(currency)) {
            result.push(currency)
          }
        }
      }

      return result
    },
  },

  methods: {
    hasCookie() {
      return typeof jQuery.cookie(this.cookieKey) !== 'undefined'
    },

    setCookie(closeAction = false) {
      jQuery.cookie(this.cookieKey, closeAction ? '0' : '1', {
        expires: 30,
        path: '/',
      })
    },

    close() {
      // Set the cookie
      this.setCookie()

      // Hide the modal
      this.canShow = false
    },

    openShop() {
      if (!this.shop) {
        return
      }

      // Set the cookie
      this.setCookie()

      // Redirect
      const shopUrlParams = this.hasCurrencySelect
        ? '?' +
          [
            `refCountry=${this.selectedCountryCode}`,
            `refCurrency=${this.selectedCurrencyCode}`,
          ].join('&')
        : ''

      window.location = `${this.shop.url}${shopUrlParams}`
    },

    async initGeoCountry() {
      if (this.geoCountry) {
        return
      }

      try {
        const url = 'https://www.ui.com/api/geoip'
        const res = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST' })
        const { country_code: code, country_name: name } = await res.json()

        // Set the country as the selected country
        this.selectedCountryCode = code
        this.geoCountry = { code, name }
      } catch (e) {
          console.error('Failed to get country. ', e)
      }
    },

    initShop() {
      if (this.shop || !this.geoCountry) {
        return
      }

      for (const shop of this.shops) {
        const hasCountry = shop.countries.some(
          ({ code }) => code === this.geoCountry.code,
        )

        if (hasCountry) {
          this.shop = shop
          break
        }
      }
    },

    handleRefParams() {
      const { origin, searchParams } = new URL(location.href)
      let reloadPage = false

      // Set country
      const refCountry = searchParams.get('refCountry')

      if (refCountry) {
        jQuery.cookie('site-country', refCountry, {
          path: '/',
        })
        reloadPage = true
      }

      // Set currency
      const refCurrency = searchParams.get('refCurrency')

      if (refCurrency) {
        jQuery.cookie('site-currency', refCurrency, {
          path: '/',
        })
        reloadPage = true
      }

      // Reload the page to update content and remove parameters
      if (reloadPage) {
        window.location = origin
      }
    },
  },

  async mounted() {
    // Init data
    await this.initGeoCountry()
    this.initShop(this.geoCountry)

    jQuery(() => {
      // Handle ref parameters
      this.handleRefParams()

      // Check if modal can be shown
      this.canShow =
        !this.hasCookie() &&
        this.geoCountry &&
        this.shop &&
        this.shop.origin !== this.currentShopOrigin
    })
  },
})
</script>

    
  </div>

  <div class="comShopHeader__mobile__menu" :class="{ 'active': show }" ref="menu">

<script type="text/javascript">
$(() => {
  let totalWIdth = 0;
  const $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems = $('#mobileShopHeaderSubmenu > li');
  $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems.each(function() { totalWIdth += $(this).width() });

  $('.comShopHeaderSubmenu .flexslider').flexslider({
    animation: 'slide',
    controlNav: false,
    animationLoop: false,
    slideshow: false,
    itemWidth: totalWIdth / $mobileShopHeaderSubmenuItems.length,
    itemMargin: 0,
    start: $slider => {
      const { pagingCount } = $slider;
      const itemIndex = $slider.find('.comShopHeaderSubmenu__item.active').index();
      const slidePageIndex = pagingCount !== 1 ? Math.floor(itemIndex / pagingCount) : 0;

      $slider.flexAnimate(slidePageIndex);
    },
  });
});
$(window).on('resize', () => {
  const flexData = jQuery('.comShopHeaderSubmenu .flexslider').data('flexslider');

  if (flexData) {
    flexData.setup();
  }
});
</script>

<script>
  const carouselApp = {
    state: {
      currentSlide: 1,
      autoRotateInterval: null,
      autoRotateDirection: 'right',

      animationTimeout: null,
      isAnimating: false,
      touchstartX: 0,
      touchendX: 0,
    },

    elements: {
      container: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_slidesContainer'),
      slides: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_slides'),
      nav: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_nav'),
      navRight: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_navRight'),
      navLeft: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_navLeft'),
      footer: document.getElementById('bannerCarousel_footer'),
    },

    // Get count of slides in carousel
    getSlidesCount() {
      return this.elements.slides.childElementCount
    },

    // Get width of the overflow container in carousel
    getContainerWidth() {
      return this.elements.container.getBoundingClientRect().width
    },

    handleGesture() {
      const { touchendX, touchstartX } = this.state
      const touchSlideDistance = (touchstartX - touchendX)

      if (touchSlideDistance < -50) {
        this.slideLeft(true)
      } else if (touchSlideDistance > 50) {
        this.slideRight(true)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(this.state.currentSlide, true)
      }
    },

    // Helper to slide one step left
    slideLeft(cancelInterval = false, clickEvent) {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { slides } = this.elements

      if (clickEvent && clickEvent.stopPropagation) {
        clickEvent.stopPropagation()
      }

      if (currentSlide > 1) {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide - 1, cancelInterval)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide)
      }
    },

    // Helper to slide one step right
    slideRight(cancelInterval = false, clickEvent) {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { slides } = this.elements

      if (clickEvent && clickEvent.stopPropagation) {
        clickEvent.stopPropagation()
      }

      if (currentSlide < this.getSlidesCount()) {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide + 1, cancelInterval)
      } else {
        this.slideTo(currentSlide)
      }
    },

    // Slide to slide number - (index 1)
    slideTo(slideNum, cancelInterval = false) {
      clearInterval(this.state.animationTimeout)
      this.state.isAnimating = true

      this.state.animationTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        this.state.isAnimating = false
      }, 800)

      if (cancelInterval) {
        clearInterval(this.state.autoRotateInterval)
      }

      const { navLeft, navRight } = this.elements

      if (slideNum === 1) {
        navLeft.classList.add('disabled')
      } else {
        navLeft.classList.remove('disabled')
      }

      if (slideNum === this.getSlidesCount()) {
        navRight.classList.add('disabled')
      } else {
        navRight.classList.remove('disabled')
      }

      this.state.currentSlide = slideNum

      const leftPos = this.getContainerWidth() * (slideNum - 1)
      this.elements.slides.style.left = `${-leftPos}px`

      this.updateActiveThumb()
    },

    // Set the static width of slides
    setSlidesWidth() {
      const { slides, container } = this.elements
      const containerWidth = this.getContainerWidth()

      this.slideTo(1)

      slides.style.width = `${containerWidth}px`
    },

    // Update thumb elements to show current active slide
    updateActiveThumb() {
      const { currentSlide } = this.state
      const { footer } = this.elements

      let i = 0
      for (const el of footer.children) {
        if (i + 1 === currentSlide) {
          el.classList.add('active')
        } else {
          el.classList.remove('active')
        }

        i += 1
      }
    },

    initSlideThumbs() {
      const { footer } = this.elements
      const indicatorHTML = `<svg width="9" height="8" viewBox="0 0 9 8" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><circle cx="4.5" cy="4" r="4" fill="#C8CAD3"/></svg>`

      for (let i = 0; i < this.getSlidesCount(); i++) {
        const el = document.createElement('button')

        el.innerHTML = indicatorHTML
        el.id = `bannerCarouselThumb_${i + 1}`
        el.classList.add('banner-carousel__thumb')

        el.addEventListener('click', () => {
          this.slideTo(i + 1, true)
        })

        footer.appendChild(el)
      }

      this.updateActiveThumb()
    },

    initInterval() {
      this.state.autoRotateInterval = setInterval(() => {
        const { currentSlide, autoRotateDirection } = this.state
        const slidesCount = this.getSlidesCount()

        if (autoRotateDirection === 'right' && currentSlide < slidesCount) {
          this.slideRight()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'right') {
          this.state.autoRotateDirection = 'left'
          this.slideLeft()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'left' && currentSlide > 1) {
          this.slideLeft()
        } else if (autoRotateDirection === 'left') {
          this.state.autoRotateDirection = 'right'
          this.slideRight()
        }
      }, 6000)
    },

    init() {
      const {
        container,
        slides,
        navRight,
        navLeft,
        nav,
      } = this.elements

      this.setSlidesWidth()
      this.initSlideThumbs()
      this.slideTo(1)
      this.initInterval()

      window.addEventListener('resize', this.setSlidesWidth.bind(this))
      navRight.addEventListener('click', () => this.slideRight.bind(this)(true, event))
      navLeft.addEventListener('click', () => this.slideLeft.bind(this)(true, event))

      /**
       * Record touchstart X positon
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
        if (this.state.isAnimating) {
          this.state.touchstartX = null
          return
        }

        slides.style.transition = 'none'
        this.state.touchstartX = e.changedTouches[0].screenX
      })

      /**
       * Visual "drag" animation
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchmove', e => {
        if (typeof this.state.touchstartX !== 'number') {
          return
        }

        const draggedDistance = e.changedTouches[0].screenX - this.state.touchstartX
        const currentSlideLeftPos = 0 - (this.getContainerWidth() * (this.state.currentSlide - 1))

        const draggedLeftPos = currentSlideLeftPos + (draggedDistance / 2)
        const minLeftPos = 0 - (this.getContainerWidth() * (this.getSlidesCount() - 1))

        if (draggedLeftPos < 0 && draggedLeftPos > minLeftPos) {
          slides.style.left = `${draggedLeftPos}px`
        }
      })

      /**
       * Record touchend X positon and check if valid gesture for carousel slide
       */
      container.addEventListener('touchend', e => {
        if (typeof this.state.touchstartX !== 'number') {
          return
        }

        slides.style.transition = 'left .8s'
        this.state.touchendX = e.changedTouches[0].screenX
        this.handleGesture()
      })

      nav.style.display = 'block'
    },
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', () => {
    carouselApp.init()
  })
</script>
